   "yadāgneyo 'ṣṭākapālo 'māvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ cācyuta" iti	"yat-AgneyaH azwAkapAlaH amAvAsyAyAm pOrNamAsyAm ca-acyuta" iti
   vākyenetyarthaḥ /	vAkyena-iti-arTaH /
   paurṇamāsyadhikaraṇe prakaraṇāntarādhikaraṇagataprakāśakāroktarītyā	pOrNamAsI-aDikaraNe prakaraNa-antara-aDikaraNa-gata-prakASa-kAra-ukta-rItyA
   prakaraṇāntarādāgneyabhedaṃ	prakaraNa-antarAt-Agneya-Bedam
   nirasyaikakarmāsaṃbhavipaurṇamāsyamāvāsyālakṣaṇaguṇadvayayogānnyāyasudhākṛdupapāditādāgneyabhedasya	nirasya-eka-karma-asaMBavi-pOrNamAsya-mAvAsyA-lakzaNa-guNa-dvaya-yogAt-nyAya-suDA-kRt-upapAditAt-Agneya-Bedasya
   svayaṃ prasādhitatvādāgneyaṃ ityekavacanamayuktamapi	svayam prasADita-tvAt-Agneyam iti-eka-vacanam-ayuktam-api
   jātyabhiprāyeṇaikavacanavivakṣayā prayuktam /	jAti-aBiprAyeNa-eka-vacana-vivakzayA prayuktam /
   śrutamiti //	Srutam-iti //
   pradeśāntara ityarthaḥ /	pradeSa-antaraH iti-arTaH /
   prakaraṇāntarāditi //	prakaraNa-antarAt-iti //
   anena ātideśikyanantarasaṅgatiḥ sūcitā /	anena Ati-deSikI-anantara-saFgatiH sUcitA /
   kathañcit sannidheḥ pratibandhakatvena prakaraṇāntarāt	kaTaQcid sanniDeH pratibanDaka-tvena prakaraNa-antarAt
   bhedāsiddhirityabhipretya tatsatve 'pi bhedakamupanyasyati ----------	Beda-asidDiH-iti-aBipretya tad-satve api Bedakam-upanyasyati ----------
   abhyāsādveti //	aByAsAt-vA-iti //
   yadyapi saṃpratipannadevatākatvena dvayorāgneyayoḥ	yadi-api saMpratipanna-devatAka-tvena dvayoH-AgneyayoH
   sahānuṣṭhānānnāgneyadvayakaraṇaprasaktiḥ pūravapakṣe; tathāpi	saha-anuzWAna-at-na-Agneya-dvaya-karaNa-prasaktiH pUrava-pakze; taTA-api
   punarvidhivaiyarthyāpattyaiva sahānuṣṭhānabādhāt, athavā ------------	punar-viDi-vEyarTya-ApattyA-eva saha-anuzWAna-bADAt, aTavA ------------
   puroḍāśadvayakaraṇādvā'gneyadvayakaraṇamabhipretyāha -------- ata eveti /	puroxASa-dvaya-karaNAt-vA-agneya-dvaya-karaNam-aBipretya-Aha ------- atas eva-iti /
   yadāgneya iti vākyāntareṇā'gneyasya kevalāgnidevatātvāvadhāraṇāt kathaṃ	yat-AgneyaH iti vAkya-antareNA-agneyasya kevala-agni-devatA-tva-avaDAraNAt kaTam
   tenaindrāgnapraśaṃsetyapekṣāyāmāha ---------- praśasteti //	tena-EndrAgna-praSaMsA-iti-apekzAyAm-Aha --------- praSastA-iti //
   "aṅgiraso vā ita uttamāḥ svargaṃlokamāyanni"	"aFgirasaH vE itas uttamAH svargaMlokam-Ayanni"
   tyādyarthavādasahitatadvidhinā āgneyaprāśastyāvagamāt	tyAdi-arTavAda-sahita-tad-viDinA Agneya-prASastya-avagamAt
   praśastāgneyasāhityenaindrāgnapraśaṃsetyarthaḥ //	praSasta-Agneya-sAhityena-EndrAgna-praSaMsA-iti-arTaH //
   pūrvapakṣe prayojanamamāvāsyāyāmāgneyadvayasya	pUrva-pakze prayojanam-amAvAsyAyAm-Agneya-dvayasya
   tatsaṃbandhitvenāṣṭākapāladvayasya karaṇaṃ, siddhānte neti	tad-saMbanDi-tvena-azwAkapAla-dvayasya karaNan, sidDAnte na-iti
   spaṣṭatvānnoktam //	spazwa-tvAt-na-uktam //
   iti caturdaśamāgneyastutyarthatādhikaraṇam //	iti caturdaSam-Agneya-stuti-arTa-tA-aDikaraNam //
   iti bhāṭṭadīpikāprabhāvalyāṃ dvitīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyāpādaḥ //	iti BAwwa-dIpikA-praBAvalyAm dvitIya-aDyAyasya tRtIyA-pAdaH //
